Claude-Mem seamlessly preserves context across sessions by automatically capturing tool usage observations, generating semantic summaries, and making them available to future sessions. This enables Claude to maintain continuity of knowledge about projects even after sessions end or reconnect.\n\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKey Features:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🧠 \u003cstrong\u003ePersistent Memory\u003c/strong\u003e - Context survives across sessions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e📊 \u003cstrong\u003eProgressive Disclosure\u003c/strong\u003e - Layered memory retrieval with token cost visibility\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🔍 \u003cstrong\u003eSkill-Based Search\u003c/strong\u003e - Query your project history with mem-search skill\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🖥️ \u003cstrong\u003eWeb Viewer UI\u003c/strong\u003e - Real-time memory stream at \u003ca href=\"http://localhost:37777\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003ehttp://localhost:37777\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e💻 \u003cstrong\u003eClaude Desktop Skill\u003c/strong\u003e - Search memory from Claude Desktop conversations\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🔒 \u003cstrong\u003ePrivacy Control\u003c/strong\u003e - Use \u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;private\u0026gt;\u003c/code\u003e tags to exclude sensitive content from storage\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e⚙️ \u003cstrong\u003eContext Configuration\u003c/strong\u003e - Fine-grained control over what context gets injected\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🤖 \u003cstrong\u003eAutomatic Operation\u003c/strong\u003e - No manual intervention required\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🔗 \u003cstrong\u003eCitations\u003c/strong\u003e - Reference past observations <p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a href="#quick-start">Quick Start</a> •
  <a href="#how-it-works">How It Works</a> •
  <a href="#mcp-search-tools">Search Tools</a> •
  <a href="#documentation">Documentation</a> •
  <a href="#configuration">Configuration</a> •
  <a href="#troubleshooting">Troubleshooting</a> •
  <a href="#license">License</a>
</p>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  Claude-Mem seamlessly preserves context across sessions by automatically capturing tool usage observations, generating semantic summaries, and making them available to future sessions. This enables Claude to maintain continuity of knowledge about projects even after sessions end or reconnect.
</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start" href="#quick-start"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Install with a single command:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npx claude-mem install"><pre>npx claude-mem install</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Or install for Gemini CLI (auto-detects <code>~/.gemini</code>):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npx claude-mem install --ide gemini-cli"><pre>npx claude-mem install --ide gemini-cli</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Or install for OpenCode:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npx claude-mem install --ide opencode"><pre>npx claude-mem install --ide opencode</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Or install from the plugin marketplace inside Claude Code:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/plugin marketplace add thedotmack/claude-mem

/plugin install claude-mem"><pre>/plugin marketplace add thedotmack/claude-mem

/plugin install claude-mem</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Restart Claude Code or Gemini CLI. Context from previous sessions will automatically appear in new sessions.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note:</strong> Claude-Mem is also published on npm, but <code>npm install -g claude-mem</code> installs the <strong>SDK/library only</strong> — it does not register the plugin hooks or set up the worker service. Always install via <code>npx claude-mem install</code> or the <code>/plugin</code> commands above.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🦞 OpenClaw Gateway</h3><a id="user-content--openclaw-gateway" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🦞 OpenClaw Gateway" href="#-openclaw-gateway"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Install claude-mem as a persistent memory plugin on <a href="https://openclaw.ai" rel="nofollow">OpenClaw</a> gateways with a single command:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -fsSL https://install.cmem.ai/openclaw.sh | bash"><pre>curl -fsSL https://install.cmem.ai/openclaw.sh <span class="pl-k">|</span> bash</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The installer handles dependencies, plugin setup, AI provider configuration, worker startup, and optional real-time observation feeds to Telegram, Discord, Slack, and more. See the <a href="https://docs.claude-mem.ai/openclaw-integration" rel="nofollow">OpenClaw Integration Guide</a> for details.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Key Features:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🧠 <strong>Persistent Memory</strong> - Context survives across sessions</li>
<li>📊 <strong>Progressive Disclosure</strong> - Layered memory retrieval with token cost visibility</li>
<li>🔍 <strong>Skill-Based Search</strong> - Query your project history with mem-search skill</li>
<li>🖥️ <strong>Web Viewer UI</strong> - Real-time memory stream at <a href="http://localhost:37777" rel="nofollow">http://localhost:37777</a></li>
<li>💻 <strong>Claude Desktop Skill</strong> - Search memory from Claude Desktop conversations</li>
<li>🔒 <strong>Privacy Control</strong> - Use <code>&lt;private&gt;</code> tags to exclude sensitive content from storage</li>
<li>⚙️ <strong>Context Configuration</strong> - Fine-grained control over what context gets injected</li>
<li>🤖 <strong>Automatic Operation</strong> - No manual intervention required</li>
<li>🔗 <strong>Citations</strong> - Reference past observations with IDs (access via <a href="http://localhost:37777/api/observation/%7Bid%7D" rel="nofollow">http://localhost:37777/api/observation/{id}</a> or view all in the web viewer at <a href="http://localhost:37777" rel="nofollow">http://localhost:37777</a>)</li>
<li>🧪 <strong>Beta Channel</strong> - Try experimental features like Endless Mode via version switching</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Documentation</h2><a id="user-content-documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Documentation" href="#documentation"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How It Works</h2><a id="user-content-how-it-works" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How It Works" href="#how-it-works"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Core Components:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>5 Lifecycle Hooks</strong> - SessionStart, UserPromptSubmit, PostToolUse, Stop, SessionEnd (6 hook scripts)</li>
<li><strong>Smart Install</strong> - Cached dependency checker (pre-hook script, not a lifecycle hook)</li>
<li><strong>Worker Service</strong> - HTTP API on port 37777 with web viewer UI and 10 search endpoints, managed by Bun</li>
<li><strong>SQLite Database</strong> - Stores sessions, observations, summaries</li>
<li><strong>mem-search Skill</strong> - Natural language queries with progressive disclosure</li>
<li><strong>Chroma Vector Database</strong> - Hybrid semantic + keyword search for intelligent context retrieval</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">See <a href="https://docs.claude-mem.ai/architecture/overview" rel="nofollow">Architecture Overview</a> for details.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">MCP Search Tools</h2><a id="user-content-mcp-search-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: MCP Search Tools" href="#mcp-search-tools"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Claude-Mem provides intelligent memory search through <strong>4 MCP tools</strong> following a token-efficient <strong>3-layer workflow pattern</strong>:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>The 3-Layer Workflow:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>search</code></strong> - Get compact index with IDs (~50-100 tokens/result)</li>
<li><strong><code>timeline</code></strong> - Get chronological context around interesting results</li>
<li><strong><code>get_observations</code></strong> - Fetch full details ONLY for filtered IDs (~500-1,000 tokens/result)</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>How It Works:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Claude uses MCP tools to search your memory</li>
<li>Start with <code>search</code> to get an index of results</li>
<li>Use <code>timeline</code> to see what was happening around specific observations</li>
<li>Use <code>get_observations</code> to fetch full details for relevant IDs</li>
<li><strong>~10x token savings</strong> by filtering before fetching details</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Available MCP Tools:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>search</code></strong> - Search memory index with full-text queries, filters by type/date/project</li>
<li><strong><code>timeline</code></strong> - Get chronological context around a specific observation or query</li>
<li><strong><code>get_observations</code></strong> - Fetch full observation details by IDs (always batch multiple IDs)</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example Usage:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Step 1: Search for index
search(query=&quot;authentication bug&quot;, type=&quot;bugfix&quot;, limit=10)

// Step 2: Review index, identify relevant IDs (e.g., #123, #456)

// Step 3: Fetch full details
get_observations(ids=[123, 456])"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Step 1: Search for index</span>
<span class="pl-en">search</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">query</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"authentication bug"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"bugfix"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">limit</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Step 2: Review index, identify relevant IDs (e.g., #123, #456)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Step 3: Fetch full details</span>
<span class="pl-en">get_observations</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">ids</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">123</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">456</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">See <a href="https://docs.claude-mem.ai/usage/search-tools" rel="nofollow">Search Tools Guide</a> for detailed examples.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Beta Features</h2><a id="user-content-beta-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Beta Features" href="#beta-features"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Claude-Mem offers a <strong>beta channel</strong> with experimental features like <strong>Endless Mode</strong> (biomimetic memory architecture for extended sessions). Switch between stable and beta versions from the web viewer UI at <a href="http://localhost:37777" rel="nofollow">http://localhost:37777</a> → Settings.</p>
<p dir="auto">See <strong><a href="https://docs.claude-mem.ai/beta-features" rel="nofollow">Beta Features Documentation</a></strong> for details on Endless Mode and how to try it.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">System Requirements</h2><a id="user-content-system-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: System Requirements" href="#system-requirements"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Node.js</strong>: 20.0.0 or higher</li>
<li><strong>Claude Code</strong>: Latest version with plugin support</li>
<li><strong>Bun</strong>: JavaScript runtime and process manager (auto-installed if missing)</li>
<li><strong>uv</strong>: Python package manager for vector search (auto-installed if missing)</li>
<li><strong>SQLite 3</strong>: For persistent storage (bundled)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Windows Setup Notes</h3><a id="user-content-windows-setup-notes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Windows Setup Notes" href="#windows-setup-notes"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you see an error like:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npm : The term 'npm' is not recognized as the name of a cmdlet"><pre>npm : The term <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>npm<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> is not recognized as the name of a cmdlet</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Make sure Node.js and npm are installed and added to your PATH. Download the latest Node.js installer from <a href="https://nodejs.org" rel="nofollow">https://nodejs.org</a> and restart your terminal after installation.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuration</h2><a id="user-content-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuration" href="#configuration"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Settings are managed in <code>~/.claude-mem/settings.json</code> (auto-created with defaults on first run). Configure AI model, worker port, data directory, log level, and context injection settings.</p>
<p dir="auto">See the <strong><a href="https://docs.claude-mem.ai/configuration" rel="nofollow">Configuration Guide</a></strong> for all available settings and examples.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mode &amp; Language Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-mode--language-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mode &amp; Language Configuration" href="#mode--language-configuration"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Claude-Mem supports multiple workflow modes and languages via the <code>CLAUDE_MEM_MODE</code> setting.</p>
<p dir="auto">This option controls both:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The workflow behavior (e.g. code, chill, investigation)</li>
<li>The language used in generated observations</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to Configure</h4><a id="user-content-how-to-configure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to Configure" href="#how-to-configure"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Edit your settings file at <code>~/.claude-mem/settings.json</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;CLAUDE_MEM_MODE&quot;: &quot;code--zh&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"CLAUDE_MEM_MODE"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>code--zh<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Modes are defined in <code>plugin/modes/</code>. To see all available modes locally:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="ls ~/.claude/plugins/marketplaces/thedotmack/plugin/modes/"><pre>ls <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.claude/plugins/marketplaces/thedotmack/plugin/modes/</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Available Modes</h4><a id="user-content-available-modes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Available Modes" href="#available-modes"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Mode</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>code</code></td>
<td>Default English mode</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>code--zh</code></td>
<td>Simplified Chinese mode</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>code--ja</code></td>
<td>Japanese mode</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">Language-specific modes follow the pattern <code>code--[lang]</code> where <code>[lang]</code> is the ISO 639-1 language code (e.g., <code>zh</code> for Chinese, <code>ja</code> for Japanese, <code>es</code> for Spanish).</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Note: <code>code--zh</code> (Simplified Chinese) is already built-in — no additional installation or plugin update is required.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">After Changing Mode</h4><a id="user-content-after-changing-mode" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: After Changing Mode" href="#after-changing-mode"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Restart Claude Code to apply the new mode configuration.</h2><a id="user-content-restart-claude-code-to-apply-the-new-mode-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Restart Claude Code to apply the new mode configuration." href="#restart-claude-code-to-apply-the-new-mode-configuration"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Development</h2><a id="user-content-development" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Development" href="#development"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">See the <strong><a href="https://docs.claude-mem.ai/development" rel="nofollow">Development Guide</a></strong> for build instructions, testing, and contribution workflow.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Troubleshooting</h2><a id="user-content-troubleshooting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Troubleshooting" href="#troubleshooting"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If experiencing issues, describe the problem to Claude and the troubleshoot skill will automatically diagnose and provide fixes.</p>
<p dir="auto">See the <strong><a href="https://docs.claude-mem.ai/troubleshooting" rel="nofollow">Troubleshooting Guide</a></strong> for common issues and solutions.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Bug Reports</h2><a id="user-content-bug-reports" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Bug Reports" href="#bug-reports"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create comprehensive bug reports with the automated generator:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd ~/.claude/plugins/marketplaces/thedotmack
npm run bug-report"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.claude/plugins/marketplaces/thedotmack
npm run bug-report</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Contributing</h2><a id="user-content-contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contributing" href="#contributing"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">License</h2><a id="user-content-license" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: License" href="#license"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Claude-Mem is licensed under the Apache License 2.0.</p>
<p dir="auto">We chose Apache-2.0 because durable agentic memory should be easy to embed in
developer tools, local agents, MCP servers, enterprise systems, robotics stacks,
and production agent harnesses.</p>
<p dir="auto">See the <a href="/thedotmack/claude-mem/blob/main/LICENSE">LICENSE</a> file for full details. See <a href="/thedotmack/claude-mem/blob/main/docs/license.md">docs/license.md</a>
and <a href="/thedotmack/claude-mem/blob/main/docs/ip-boundary.md">docs/ip-boundary.md</a> for licensing scope and the
open/commercial boundary.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note on Ragtime</strong>: The <code>ragtime/</code> directory is licensed under the <strong>Apache License 2.0</strong>. See <a href="/thedotmack/claude-mem/blob/main/ragtime/LICENSE">ragtime/LICENSE</a> for details.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What About CMEM?</h3><a id="user-content-what-about-cmem" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What About CMEM?" href="#what-about-cmem"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">CMEM is a token created by a 3rd party but officially embraced by the creator of Claude-Mem (Alex Newman, @thedotmack). The token acts as a community catalyst for growth and a vehicle for bringing CMEM to the developers and knowledge workers that need it most.</p>
<p dir="auto">Official BASE CA: 0x76b1967eec0ccaeb001bbbb2b40dc4badba31ba3</p>
